 After the couple's murder, questions have been raised again about the safety of the elderly in the capital
 ek aankade ke mutabik, rajdhani dilli main yun to kareeb 12 lakh bujurg hai
 But out of this, 36 thousand elderly living alone have registration with the police
 bataaya jaataa he ki jis bujurg danpati kii hatya hui, unka police ke paas panjikaran nahin tha
 Delhi Police has made registration arrangements to provide security to the elderly living alone
 police aise logon kaa samay-samay par haalchaal leti rahati he
 How to register: The Delhi Police formed the Senior Citizens Security Cell in 2004 after the increasing incidence of crime against single-aged elders
 makasad rahaa ki akele rah rahe bujurgon kii pahchaan kar unki suraksha kaa dhyaan rakhaa jaae
 Currently, the cell is operational in 15 districts of Delhi
 akele rahane vaale bujurg dilli police ke senior citigens security cell main bujurg online or ofline apana registration kara sakate hai
 Currently 36,481 elderly are registered
 dilli police 2016 main ek mobile ap bhi launch kar chuki he
 You can fill the entire bio data by downloading the Senior Police Mobile App of the Delhi Police
 jiske baad sthaneey police aavedan kii jaanch karegi

" yuvaraj inamen se ek he or hamaare paas viraat kohli, rohit sharma or suresh raina hai
